And on that one day, under the leadership of Jinnah and others, the struggle for Pakistan started with full force and it ended with the creation of Pakistan. 

On Pakistan Day, may Allah bless us with integrity to be proud of our country and may we understand the true meaning of resolution and steadfastness this day.

23/03/2022, 8:29 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: *BLOOD DONATION CAMP - UET NEW CAMPUS*
"A donation of blood means a few minutes to you, but a lifetime for somebody else."

Voluntary and unpaid regular blood donation is an act of solidarity and is required all over the world.According to WHO, many developing countries face severe shortage of blood. "The need for blood is universal, but access to blood for all those who need it is not,"

In order to raise awareness and to meet the needs of blood donations, BDS and it's team is arranging BLOOD CAMP at Health Clinic UET New Campus soon. It's the first time that a Blood Donation Camp is being arranged in our university, so each one of you is encouraged and invited to contribute, donate and volunteer in this camp. It's a deed that serves both the donor and recipient!

Donating blood is a divine experience, try it at least once in your lifetime!

Health is a gift which money cannot buy. It's your *McGuffin* . Your life depends on it. We are living in a very fast age of internet and cyberspace, in which all of our tasks could be performed within a click but health comes on the contrary. It requires your time and dedication.
In recent years, the average life expectancy in Pakistan is decreasing gradually. Heart diseases and Obesity is spreading like fire among young people.

A life without health is like a river without running water. Make yourself consistent. Have some exercise and meditate, let your body and mind heal. Have a good laugh and long sleep. Do things that your future self will thank you for.

A fit and healthy body is the best fashion statement.

“What drains your spirit, drains your body. What fuels your spirit, fuels your body.” – Carolyn Myss .

10/04/2022, 8:54 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: Ramadan is a month that symbolises sacrifice, giving for the needs of people around us.

In this Holy Month when the reward for every good deed is tenfold your single blood donation can save up to three lives. There is a misconception being built in our society that one can not donate blood during Ramadan when in reality it is medically proven that blood can be donated after the fasting hours and it means no harm to the health of the donor but adds to his rewards that are eventually going to benefit him in the world hereafter.

16/04/2022, 1:30 am - Syed Muhammad Ali 2: درد دل کے واسطے پیدا کیا انسان کو
ورنہ طاعت کے لیے کچھ کم نہ تھے کر و بیاں
She was named “The Mother of Pakistan”, by which she acted accordingly with all her soul. Alongside her husband, Builquis Bano Edhi served humanity without any discrimination of race or religion. She was the Co- chairman of Edhi foundation and an active patron of society.
Despite her husband; Andul Sattar Edhi being received by Presidents and her own appearance on Pakistani television the couple lived modestly in a two-room apartment which is part of one of their orphanages.
She received many international and national awards due to her definite and firm character and her enthusiasm to help humanity. Builquis Bano holds the honour to receive the prestigious  Hilal-i-Imtiaz, which is the highest degree award of service to the state.In 2015, she received the Mother Teresa Memorial International Award for Social Justice.
Indeed her departure had left a void space in Pakistan philanthropist society and her character would always be remembered in the history of Pakistan.It is true, as the saying goes: “There is a woman behind every man”. Bilquis Bano proved it right with all her might.

He was born in Kaaba, Makkah. He was his cousin, son-in-law, companion and raised by Prophet Muhammad ﷺ himself. He was one of the first believers of Islam. He helped Muhammadﷺ emigrate on the night of Laylat al-Mabit, by sleeping in his place. He was Murtaza (the chosen one), Asadullah( lion of Allah), Amir al-Mu'minin (prince of the faithful) and Mawla al-Mottaqin (master of the God-fearing) 

He is Ali ibn Ali Talib R.A, the Fourth Caliph of Islam. He was the last ruler amongst the Khulafa-e-Rashideen. Today marks the martyrdom of Mola Ali Sher-e-Khuda in the city of Kufa (present day Iraq).
Prophet Muhammad ﷺ  bestowed him upon the title "Path to knowledge".
The path of his character and traits is the Holy grail for Muslims all across the world. 

There was a prophecy of Hazrat Muhammad  ﷺ about Maula Ali that stated: 

"پچھلی امتوں کا سب سےبڑا بد بخت انسان وہ تھا جس نے حضرت صالح علیہ السلام کی اونٹنی کو قتل کیا۔ میری امت کا بد ترین شخص وہ ہوگا جو تیرے سر کے خون سے تیری داڑھی کو تر کر دے گا۔"

28/04/2022, 8:28 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: <Media omitted>
28/04/2022, 8:28 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: اکثر شام کو آتی ہے فلک سے آواز
سجدہ کرتی ہے جس کو سحر وہ ہے آج کی رات 

Shab-e- Qadr, also known as Laylat al-Qadr, commemorates the day that the verses of the Quran were first revealed to Prophet Muhammad (PBUH). It is considered to be one of the holiest nights of the Islamic faith. To commemorate the day, Muslims recite the verses from the Quran the entire night. 

BDS and its team urge you all to pray for the betterment of the Muslims all over the world as this night is better than 1000 months.

World ASTHMA DAY
World asthma day is organised by Global Initiative for Asthma of WHO collaborative organisation founded in 1993 .
The day was created to promote awareness of asthma as a condition that increasing. Infact it affects at least 14% of children worldwide and seems to be growing prevalence .By 2016, the World Health Organisation recognise asthma as a major public health importance.
Let us promise ourselves to take more precautions from asthma and to have surroundings that are clear and free from toxins.

BDS is a society where i have learned the real purpose of my life. i still remember the day when i and @923451406343 were at hostel and he insisted to me to join BDS, I was little confused but things started to change when i arranged first donor for Blood Donation. Duas and pleasure i recieved from them brought a huge impact on my life. Boom!  from the very next day i realized the thing what i really want to do, and Alhumdulillah! Now i'm an active social worker. I love to help the people in need, cos it gives me immense pleasure. BDS will remain always closest to my heart. We as a team worked harder to Uplifting BDS in campus. I specially want to mention *Usman* and @923451406343 here because at start we were just 3. We worked when there were few members, and the existing members did nothing 🙂. Alhumdulillah After 1 year it is best society of campus. Because we do much much more than other societies in the whole year. Now we are well established. Im gonna sign off from my position with heavy heart. its an emotional moment for me to leave BDS. I hope you guys will work as a team and continue the legacy of BDS. Finger crossed, Hoping for the Best!
*Abdullah Khan*
Blood Manager BDS UET New Campus 2020-2021
Allah Hafiz!

31/05/2022, 1:23 pm - Muzzamil Khan Cs 20: Every year, on 31 May, the World Health Organization (WHO) and global partners celebrate World No Tobacco Day (WNTD). The annual campaign is an opportunity to raise awareness on the harmful and deadly effects of tobacco use and second-hand smoke exposure, and to discourage the use of tobacco in any form.
The focus of World No Tobacco Day 2019 is on "tobacco and lung health." The campaign will increase awareness on:
the negative impact that tobacco has on people’s lung health, from cancer to chronic respiratory disease,
the fundamental role lungs play for the health and well-being of all people.
BDS and it's team urges you to quit smoking in order to live a long and healthy life.

12/06/2022, 1:17 pm - +92 301 2999008: The World Day Against Child Labour, which is held every year on June 12, is intended to foster the worldwide movement against child labour.The World Day Against Child Labour is an International Labour Organization (ILO)-sanctioned holidayfirst launched in 2002 to raise awareness and activism to prevent child labour. It was spurred by ratifications of ILO Convention No. 138 on the minimum age for employment and ILO Convention No. 182 on the worst forms of child labour.
Significance of World Against Child Labor Day is that, it  day mainly focuses on the development of children and it protects the right to education and dignified life for the children. 
BDS want people to raise awareness about child labor beacuse It is a serious problem in pakistan. Many  children in pakistan are deprive  of education and blessed childhood so we are aiming to help such children.

19/06/2022, 12:11 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: <Media omitted>
19/06/2022, 12:11 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: Our dads will always be our heroes. Convey that to him with one of these caring and inspirational Father’s Day greetings to make him feel like the best Dad ever. Fathers somehow have this magical ability to make you feel better about anything. When mom says no, you can somehow always convince dad to try to get her to change her mind — and no matter how much he rolls his eyes, he’s usually always ready to give you those few extra bucks you need. So it’s only right you shower him with lots of love on Father’s Day 2022, which falls on Sunday, June 19 this year.
BDS and it's team urges you to love, respect and take care of your father.

 *World sickle cell day post* . LIKE, SHARE AND COMMENT as much as you can do✨
19/06/2022, 5:21 pm - Muzzamil Khan Cs 20: Every year, on June 19, countries all over the world celebrate world sickle cell day, which was initially presented as a resolution by the United Nations in 2008. 

Sickle cell disease is an inherited blood disorder that causes "sickle" shaped blood cells that can stick together, blocking blood flow and oxygen from reaching all parts of the body.
The goal of this day is to recognize sickle cell anemia is a public health problem and promote education about the genetic condition.
Let us all educate ourselves and others about the disease as the 19th of June comes closer.

🩸Caption credits: 
Maryam Rafique 

🩸Graphic credits:
Muhammad Samiullah

Though Team BDS is sad as the time to say goodbye to its passing out hierarchy has arrived, but, at the same time, we are extremely grateful and thankful for the work they have done for humanity. They have done extreme justice to the famous saying 
“Apne liye to Sab hi Jeete hain Is Jehan mai 
Hai Zindagi ka Maqsad Auron ke Kaam Ana”
They have proved that heroes are not born with a silver spoon, they are from us who endows their whole life for humanity. 

Team BDS UET New Campus wishes them best of luck for their future endeavours and send them off with a bouquet of prayers and wishes and also promise to continue their legacy in serving the humanity.

01/07/2022, 2:19 pm - Muzzamil Khan Cs 20: "When there are tears, you are a Shoulder. When there is pain, you are a Medicine. When there is a tragedy, you are a Hope."
Happy Doctor's Day; 
Celebrating our heroes on July 1st, a day dedicated to doctors who stake their own lives to save others. Doctors are always important people in everyone's lives. When we need help with our health, we go to the doctor, and since the Coronavirus, doctors have become heroes and superheroes. The world has recently learned how doctors contribute to society. While we were isolated, doctors were constantly fighting for the lives of infected people. Doctors are doing everything they can to deal with the pandemic and help patients recover. They are, without a doubt, the greatest hero of all time.
BDS appreciates your commitment to providing excellence!
Wishing each one of you a happy & healthy Doctors’ Day!

02/07/2022, 7:50 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: //Monthly Report May-June '22//

"Donating blood is an act of solidarity." 
Giving blood saves lives. The blood you give is a lifeline in an emergency and for people who need long-term treatments. 

We highly appreciate  all the donors for their kindness and for taking the time to make a blood donation. We, Red army, thank you from the bottom of our beating hearts for your selfless gift. It will go a long way as you have given someone a lifeline, just at the right time.
We appreciate dedications and  tremendous efforts of every BDS member who played their role in making this achievement in the past two months.

13/07/2022, 10:57 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: *ANNOUNCEMENT*
Assalam Alaikum Everyone,

Hope this message find you all in good health. This message concerns everyone in the society. This group consists more than 100 members but only a bunch of us are actively working for the cause. Our management team has decided to change that. 

In order to make every single one of you take part in arranging blood, the blood management team has set up a task for you. Each of you will have to *register at least 3 donors in BDS records* ( it can be a friend outside of university, a relative or a person you know who's willing to donate or has donated in past). Everyone will receive a format from our team members that you'll have to fill. 

At the end of the day, the purpose of every member in this society is to help arrange blood for patients in need. 

This is just one way to know that you are trying and showing efforts, *in case if any of you do not even respond to the message/task given by our management members we'll assume you do not want to be a part of this society and will be terminated.* We hope you guys will do your best and cooperate with our team!

Regards, 
Fatima Faheem
President BDS UET New Campus

30/07/2022, 8:37 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: وابستہ ذات ہے جو شہہِ مشرقین سے
آغازِ سال کرتا ہوں نامِ حسین (رض) سے ۔
Muslims across the world are going to celebrate the Hijri new Islamic Year.
The customs of Awal Muharram vary from country to country, though they generally involve attending various religious activities, spiritual singing and religious meetings. The traditions and customs for Muharram also vary between Shia and Sunni Muslims.

For both, the marking of the beginning of the new year is usually quiet, unlike New Year's celebrations associated with other calendars. It is a time for Muslims to reflect on the passing of time and their own mortality.
BDS and it's team urge you to change yourself, and let's plug today to donate maximum blood donations for Humanities.

09/08/2022, 1:55 pm - Muzzamil Khan Cs 20: Everyone share it on your statuses and admire the great sacrifice in the course of Islamic history of our beloved Hazrat Imam Hussain Shaheed (R.A) 
"Death with dignity is better than a life of humiliation",  Imam Hussain (R.A).
09/08/2022, 1:58 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: “Qatl-e-Hussain (A.S) asal mein marg-e-yazeed hai
Islam zinda hota hai har karbala ke baad”——Maulana Mohammad Ali Jauhar

Literally meaning ‘the tenth’, Youm-e-Ashura marks the 10th day of the month of Muharram.
The Martyrdom of Imam Hussain(A.S), the grandson of the Prophet of Islam, occurred on the 10th of Muharram, the first month of the Islamic calendar (Aug 9th, 2022). Muslims worldwide commemorate that tragic event on this day on 680 AD. It was a battle between good and evil. Imam Hussain, the beloved grandson of Prophet Muhammed (peace be upon him), stood up against Yazid, who was made caliph (Khalifah) by his father, Amir Muawiyya. Yazid was an impious person who did not show Islamic character or behavior to be a Khalifah. Imam Hussain refused to recognize or endorse his leadership over the rapidly growing Muslim Ummah and Muslim state. If there’s one sacrifice that is lamented world across and rightfully so, it is that of Hussain (RA) and his family that stood up against the tyrannical rule of Yazid. Commemorated worldwide as The Great Sacrifice, Ashura brings with it a reminder of Hussain’s life and principles that he fought for.

Truth is for living and falsehood is for perishing. Team BDS UET(New Campus) pays tribute to the martyrs of Islam who stood firm and steadfast against the falsehood and evil and fought bravely till their last breaths.

Caption credits: Hammad Israr
Graphic credits: Muhammad Sami

26/08/2022, 1:42 pm - Fatima Sis BDS: //Women's Equality Day//

“When girls are educated, their countries become stronger and more prosperous.” 
- Michelle Obama
Women's Equality Day  is celebrated on August 26 and marks a turning point in the history of the struggle for equal treatment of women and women's rights.
Women's Equality Day is so significant because it promotes a sense of solidarity that makes the women's movement all the more powerful. When women work together to recognize and uplift each other in a way that emphasizes intersectionality and the freedoms that women in every walk of life deserve, change happens. 
A woman can be anything she wants as long as she decides to never fear anyone. Women are the world's greatest inspiration.  

This Women's Equality Day, BDS thank all those faceless, loud voices  who are fighting for the women's rights and work besides men for prosperity of the country.

Bushra Eman
